        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }

     <img src="/Images/media.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>Get Tech Support for Your Classroom</h3> 
      <p>Contact Multimedia Technologies at (951) 827-3041 or <a href="mailto:multimedia@ucr.edu">multimedia@ucr.edu</a> for help with:</p> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>Equipment training (how to use projectors, microphones, etc.)</li> 
       <li>Before-or-after-hours usage (using technology in your room outside of class hours)</li> 
       <li>Reserving special equipment (portable equipment that can come to you)</li> 
       <li>Technical difficulties (including network issues)</li> 
       <li>Early media set-up for one-time events</li> 
      </ul> 
     </div>

        <li><a href="http://rspace.ucr.edu">R'Space</a></li>

     <div class="span-17 last"> 
      <p>Visit <a href="http://classrooms.ucr.edu/index.php">Smart Classrooms</a> to see media technology available in each general assignment classroom.</p> 
      <p>To request a classroom with specific technology for ongoing academic activities (lectures, etc.), please see <a href="scheduling-academic-course-activities.aspx">Scheduling Academic Course Activities</a>.</p> 
      <h3>Make Classroom Maintenance Requests</h3> 
      <br /> 
      <label>Fix Temperature or Cleaning Issues</label> 
      <p>Classroom too cold? Too hot? Chalkboard or floor dirty?</p> 
      <ul>
       <li> 1. Log into <a href="http://rspace.ucr.edu">R'Space</a></li> 
       <li>2. Scroll to the Tools box</li> 
       <li>3. Click Trouble Tickets</li> 
       <li>4. Click link “Submit a Physical Plant trouble ticket” </li> 
       <p>You can also call (951) 827-3408 and we will submit a trouble ticket on your behalf.</p> 
       <label>Report Items Missing or Broken</label> 
       <p>Desks missing? Blinds or windows broken? Call us at (951) 827-3408 and we will submit a work order to <a href="http://pplant.ucr.edu/">Physical Plant</a> on your behalf. </p> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
      </ul>
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>

     <ul class="big_links"> 
      <li style="border-top: none;"><a href="/scs"><img src="/images/scs_small.jpg" alt="Student Computing Services" width="131" height="68" /><strong>Visit the SCS Website</strong>Student Computing Services is dedicated to providing technical tools &amp; support to UCR's diverse student population. Through campus computer labs, iLearn, R'Mail and much more, SCS provides the tools students need to succeed in UCR's unique academic &amp; research environment.</a></li> 
     </ul> 
     <h3>About SCS</h3> 
     <p>Student Computing Services (SCS) supports 10 student computer labs, including 7 public labs and 3 non public labs, with approximately 160 public lab hours per week (with reduced hours during breaks and summer). Additionally, we support a student laptop checkout program of 114 laptops available through the Front Desk and Latitude 55 in the Highlander Union Building (HUB), as well as the Campus Store Lounge.</p> 
     <p>SCS staff provide assistance with use of the computer labs, student email (and related Google services), iLearn, wireless network access, VPN, and other services used by UCR students. Assistance is available by:</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Coming to any of our public computer labs during open hours</li> 
      <li>Stopping by the Bear Help support desk in the HUB front lobby</li> 
      <li>Calling (951) 827-6495</li> 
      <li>Emailing helpdesk@student.ucr.edu</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p>We employ three full time staff, and approximately 25 trained Lab Consultants, to assist students with the use of our services.</p> 
     <h3>Mission Statement</h3> 
     <p>Student Computing Services strives to offer UCR students the highest level of computer services and facilities. Our primary mission - to support instruction and students with the tools and technologies necessary for classwork and research - is facilitated by:</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Providing courteous customer service</li> 
      <li>Providing the highest level of basic assistance to those who use our services</li> 
      <li>Maintaining equipment and software at the highest possible standard and striving for a maximum down-time of 48 hours</li> 
      <li>Maintaining a clean and friendly computing environment for all who use our facilities</li> 
     </ul> 
     <div class="spotlight"> 
      <h3>Contact Information</h3> 
      <p><strong>Student Computing Services</strong><br /> 2103 Watkins Hall <br />Tel: (951) 827-6495 <br />Fax: (951) 827-2726 <br />E-mail: <a href="mailto:helpdesk@student.ucr.edu?subject=Helpdesk%20Inquiry">helpdesk@student.ucr.edu </a></p> 
     </div>
